	name = TUR_armenian_population_230
	text = {
		trigger = {
			230 = {
				check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 }
				TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_subject_vilayet = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

defined_text = {
	name = TUR_jewish_state_454
	text = {
		trigger = {
			454 = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_jewish_state
				TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_subject_vilayet = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_jewish_state_political_power_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_state_political_power_factor = 0 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = TUR_jewish_state_454_yes
	}
}
